add_namespace = Ntribes
#add_namespace = Ntribes_news

country_event = { # Up to agrarian (start)
	id = Ntribes.1
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.1"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				add_political_power = 75
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NTR_steps_towards_centralization
				add_idea = NTR_uncompleted_centralization
			}
			
			add_ideas = NTR_society_increase_upkeep
			
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.2
				days = 60
				random = 240
			}
			
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.991
				days = 30
				random = 120
			}
			
			country_event = Ntribes.592
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.1.t
	desc = Ntribes.1.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.1.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				add_political_power = 75
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NTR_steps_towards_centralization
				add_idea = NTR_uncompleted_centralization
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Up to agrarian (continue)
	id = Ntribes.2
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.2"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				add_political_power = 50
			}
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_uncompleted_centralization # fascism #???
			
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.3
				days = 120
				random = 480
			}
			
			country_event = Ntribes.592
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.2.t
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = communism }
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.2.d_a
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.2.d_b
	}
	
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
		
		has_idea = communal_society
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.2.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				add_political_power = 50
			}
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_uncompleted_centralization
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = communal_society
				add_idea = communal_society1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Up to agrarian (end)
	id = Ntribes.3
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.3"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				add_political_power = 50
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = communal_society1
				add_idea = agrarian_society
			}
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_society_increase_upkeep
			
			country_event = Ntribes.592
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_poverty = yes
				}
				
				set_country_flag = can_improve_poverty
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.3.t
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_government = democratic
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.3.d_a
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.3.d_b
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_government = fascism
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.3.d_c
	}
	
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
		
		has_idea = communal_society1
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.3.a
		
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = fascism }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.025
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.025
			}
		}
		
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = communal_society1
			add_idea = agrarian_society
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_poverty = yes
			}
			
			unlock_decision_tooltip = improve_poverty_decision
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.3.b
		
		trigger = {
			has_government = fascism
		}
		
		add_political_power = 50
		
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = communal_society1
			add_idea = agrarian_society
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_poverty = yes
			}
			
			unlock_decision_tooltip = improve_poverty_decision
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Choose investor (VED, FAW or others)
	id = Ntribes.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.4" }
	title = Ntribes.4.t
	desc = Ntribes.4.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # VED
		name = Ntribes.4.a
		
		trigger = {
			VED = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
				has_government = democratic
				
				is_not_a_potential_enemy_and_has_not_war_with_ROOT = yes
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = TRADE
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		add_political_power = -50
		
		add_ideas = NTR_VED_science_base_investments
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { # 80-100
				id = Ntribes.7
				days = 80
				random = 480
			}
			
			VED = {
				country_event = Ntribes.50
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # FAW
		name = Ntribes.4.b
		
		trigger = {
			FAW = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
				has_government = democratic
				
				is_not_a_potential_enemy_and_has_not_war_with_ROOT = yes
				
				NOT = { country_exists = FAT }
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				
				VED = {
					OR = {
						exists = no
						is_subject = yes
						NOT = { has_government = democratic }
						
						is_a_potential_enemy_or_has_war_with_ROOT = yes
					}
				}
				
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = VEDINA
					}
					
					AND = {
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = TRADE
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		add_political_power = -50
		
		add_ideas = NTR_FAW_science_base_investments
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { # 80-100
				id = Ntribes.7
				days = 80
				random = 480
			}
			
			FAW = {
				country_event = Ntribes.50
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Others
		name = Ntribes.4.c
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				OR = {
					VED = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject = no
						has_government = democratic
						
						is_not_a_potential_enemy_and_has_not_war_with_ROOT = yes
					}
					
					FAW = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject = no
						has_government = democratic
						
						is_not_a_potential_enemy_and_has_not_war_with_ROOT = yes
						
						NOT = { country_exists = FAT }
					}
				}
				
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = VEDINA
					}
					
					AND = {
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		add_political_power = -75
		
		add_ideas = NTR_science_base_investments_from_dem
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { # 120-150
				id = Ntribes.7
				days = 120
				random = 720
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The First Scientists
	id = Ntribes.7
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.7"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = poor_science_base
				add_idea = better_science_base
			}
			
			set_country_flag = better_science_base_unlocked
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = NTR_science_base_investments_from_dem
					}
					
					remove_ideas = NTR_science_base_investments_from_dem
				}
				
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = NTR_VED_science_base_investments
					}
					
					remove_ideas = NTR_VED_science_base_investments
					
					VED = {
						country_event = Ntribes.52
					}
				}
				
				else = {
					remove_ideas = NTR_FAW_science_base_investments
					
					FAW = {
						country_event = Ntribes.52
					}
				}
			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = NTR_SRS_science_base_investments
				}
				
				remove_ideas = NTR_SRS_science_base_investments
				
				SRS = {
					country_event = Ntribes.52
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				remove_ideas = NTR_science_base_commie_solo_develop
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.7.t
	desc = Ntribes.7.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = democratic
			has_government = communism
		}
		
		has_idea = poor_science_base
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.7.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = poor_science_base
				add_idea = better_science_base
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = NTR_science_base_investments_from_dem
					}
					
					remove_ideas = NTR_science_base_investments_from_dem
				}
				
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = NTR_VED_science_base_investments
					}
					
					remove_ideas = NTR_VED_science_base_investments
					
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = VED
						modifier = NTR_helped_in_the_development
					}
				}
				
				else = {
					remove_ideas = NTR_FAW_science_base_investments
					
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = FAW
						modifier = NTR_helped_in_the_development
					}
				}
			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = NTR_SRS_science_base_investments
				}
				
				remove_ideas = NTR_SRS_science_base_investments
				
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = SRS
					modifier = NTR_helped_in_the_development
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				remove_ideas = NTR_science_base_commie_solo_develop
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Literacy for All
	id = Ntribes.8
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.8" }
	title = Ntribes.8.t
	desc = Ntribes.8.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # There is still a place for the elders
		name = Ntribes.8.a
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
		
		add_political_power = -75
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { # 60-70
				id = Ntribes.9
				days = 60
				random = 240
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # We must go all the way
		name = Ntribes.8.b
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				
				has_government = democratic
			}
		}
		
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -150
		
		country_event = { # 90-105
			id = Ntribes.9
			days = 90
			random = 360
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NTR_new_education_doctrine
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Making Progress
	id = Ntribes.9
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.9"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = lack_of_scientists 
				add_idea = lack_of_scientists1
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_new_education_doctrine
				}
				
				country_event = {
					id = Ntribes.10
					days = 90
					random = 360
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = Ntribes.10
					days = 60
					random = 240
				}
			}
			
			country_event = Ntribes.592
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.9.t
	desc = Ntribes.9.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = democratic
			has_government = communism
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.9.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = lack_of_scientists 
				add_idea = lack_of_scientists1
			}
		}
	}
}

				}

					popularity = 0.02

					random = 24
				}
			}

			NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_FROM_effect = yes
			
			FROM = {
				country_event = Ntribes.56
			}
			
			country_event = Ntribes.592
		}

				popularity = 0.02

	}

	id = Ntribes.16
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.16"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				
				add_political_power = -50
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_FROM_effect = yes
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.02
				}
				
				FROM = {
					country_event = Ntribes.56
				}
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = agrarian_society6
				add_idea = pre_industrial_society
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_poverty = yes
				}
				
				hidden_effect = {
					set_country_flag = can_improve_poverty
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_not_completed
				}
				
				clr_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_not_completed
			}
			
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_helper
				}
				
				clr_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_helper
			}
			
			country_event = Ntribes.592
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.16.t
	desc = Ntribes.16.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.16.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				
				add_political_power = -50
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_FROM_effect = yes
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.02
				}
			}
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = agrarian_society6
				add_idea = pre_industrial_society
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_poverty = yes
			}
			
			unlock_decision_tooltip = improve_poverty_decision
		}
	}
}

				limit = {
					has_idea = FAW_NTR_science_base_investment
				}

			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = VED
				}

			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					tag = FAW
				}
				
				remove_ideas = FAW_NTR_science_base_investment
			}
			
			else = {
				remove_ideas = SRS_NTR_science_base_investments
			}
			
			FROM = {

					target = ROOT
					modifier = NTR_helped_in_the_development
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # Request for help
	id = Ntribes.53
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.53" }
	title = Ntribes.53.t
	desc = Ntribes.53.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # Accept
		name = Ntribes.53.a
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
		}
		
		add_political_power = 50
		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.025
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				set_country_flag = NTR_VED_up_to_pre_industrial_helper
				
				country_event = Ntribes.12
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Reject
		name = Ntribes.53.b
		
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_ai = no
						
						has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = VEDINA
						}
						
						AND = {
							is_historical_focus_on = yes
							
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = NTR_ai_behavior
								option = DEFAULT
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		add_political_power = -25
		add_stability = -0.025
		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = Ntribes.13
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

	}

country_event = { # Call from the North
	id = Ntribes.55
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.55" }
	title = Ntribes.55.t
	desc = Ntribes.55.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = { # Of course we will help them!
		name = Ntribes.55.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = modern_society
			}
			
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = agrarian_society6
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = communism
						}
						
						country_event = { # ~60
							id = Ntribes.18
							days = 55
							random = 240
						}
					}
					
					else = {
						country_event = { # ~60
							id = Ntribes.16
							days = 55
							random = 240
						}
					}
				}
				
				else = {
					country_event = { # ~60
						id = Ntribes.15
						days = 55
						random = 240
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = outdated_industry
			}
			
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = agrarian_society6
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = communism
						}
						
						country_event = { # ~75
							id = Ntribes.18
							days = 70
							random = 240
						}
					}
					
					else = {
						country_event = { # ~75
							id = Ntribes.16
							days = 70
							random = 240
						}
					}
				}
				
				else = {
					country_event = { # ~75
						id = Ntribes.15
						days = 70
						random = 240
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = agrarian_society6
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = communism
						}
						
						country_event = { # ~90
							id = Ntribes.18
							days = 85
							random = 240
						}
					}
					
					else = {
						country_event = { # ~90
							id = Ntribes.16
							days = 85
							random = 240
						}
					}
				}
				
				else = {
					country_event = { # ~90
						id = Ntribes.15
						days = 85
						random = 240
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_helper
			
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_potential_helper
				}
				
				clr_country_flag = NTR_potential_helper
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # *Autistic speech*
		name = Ntribes.55.b
		
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			
			FROM = {
				NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_autists
			
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = democratic
					}
					
					country_event = Ntribes.98
				}
				
				else = {
					country_event = Ntribes.96
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Up to Outdated Society (gradations checks)
	id = Ntribes.95
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.95" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = has_outdated_industry_flag
	}
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = pre_industrial_society3 }
			}
			
			increase_society_development_gradual = yes
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = neutrality
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
				
				country_event = { # for neu
					id = Ntribes.95
					days = 90
					random = 360
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				country_event = { # for dem and com
					id = Ntribes.95
					days = 70
					random = 280
				}
			}
		}
		
		else_if = { # for all
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government = fascism }
			}
			
			country_event = Ntribes.22
		}
		
		else = {
			country_event = Ntribes.411
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #	Calculation for 'Help from Comrades'
	id = Ntribes.96
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.96" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_other_country = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_potential_helper
					
					NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_autists }
				}
			}
			
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_potential_helper
					
					NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_autists }
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.55
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_other_country = {
					exists = yes
					has_war = no
					has_government = communism
					
					OR = {
						has_idea = pre_industrial_society
						has_idea = outdated_industry
						has_idea = modern_society
					}
					
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_autists
						
						has_or_is_justifying_wargoal_against_ROOT = yes
						
						ROOT = {
							OR = {
								has_wargoal_against = PREV
								is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					exists = yes
					has_war = no
					has_government = communism
					
					OR = {
						has_idea = pre_industrial_society
						has_idea = outdated_industry
						has_idea = modern_society
					}
					
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_autists
						
						has_or_is_justifying_wargoal_against_ROOT = yes
						
						ROOT = {
							OR = {
								has_wargoal_against = PREV
								is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
				
				set_country_flag = NTR_potential_helper
			}
			
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_potential_helper
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.55
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.15
				days = 120
				random = 480
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #	Calculation for 'Trade with SRS'
	id = Ntribes.97
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.97" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = democratic
			has_government = communism
		}
		
		OR = {
			has_idea = agrarian_society2
			has_idea = agrarian_society3
			has_idea = agrarian_society4
			has_idea = agrarian_society5
			has_idea = agrarian_society6
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war = no
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						SRS = {
							exists = yes
							is_subject = no
							has_government = communism
							
							has_war = no
							has_civil_war = no
							
							NOT = {
								has_or_is_justifying_wargoal_against_ROOT = yes
								
								ROOT = {
									OR = {
										has_wargoal_against = PREV
										is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = agrarian_society6
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.18
					}
					
					else = {
						country_event = Ntribes.17
					}
					
					SRS = {
						country_event = Ntribes.57
					}
				}
			}
			
			else = { # wait
				set_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_not_completed
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			country_event = Ntribes.98
		}
	}
}

			has_government = communism
		}
		
		OR = {
			has_idea = agrarian_society2
			has_idea = agrarian_society3
			has_idea = agrarian_society4
			has_idea = agrarian_society5
			has_idea = agrarian_society6
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = no

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}

					has_war = no
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						VED = {
							exists = yes
							has_war = no
							is_subject = no
							has_government = democratic
							
							NOT = {
								has_or_is_justifying_wargoal_against_ROOT = yes
								
								ROOT = {
									OR = {
										has_wargoal_against = PREV
										is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = agrarian_society6
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.14
					}
					
					else = {
						country_event = Ntribes.16
					}
					
					VED = {
						country_event = Ntribes.54
					}
				}
				
				else = { # to "Trade with All"
					country_event = Ntribes.98
				}
			}
			
			else = { # wait
				set_country_flag = NTR_up_to_pre_industrial_not_completed
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			country_event = Ntribes.97
		}
	}
}

	id = Ntribes.100

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # The last say in all decisions will rest with me
		name = Ntribes.100.a
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				VED = {
					OR = {
						exists = no
						is_subject = yes
						
						NOT = {
							has_government = democratic
						}
					}
				}
				
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = TRADE
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = 0.075
		
		add_ideas = NTR_an_executive_monarchy
		
		set_cosmetic_tag = NTR_queen
	}
	
	option = { # The last say rests with the representatives of the tribes
		name = Ntribes.100.b
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				VED = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject = no
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = VEDINA
					}
					
					AND = {
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		add_stability = -0.05
		
		add_ideas = NTR_a_constitutional_monarchy

			ideology = democratic
			long_name = NTR_liberal_party_long
			name = NTR_liberal_party
		}
		
		set_cosmetic_tag = NTR_trade
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_leader_ideology = liberalism
		}
	}
}

		name = Ntribes.162.a
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				
				check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = -1 }
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				
				check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = -2 }
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				
				check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = -3 }
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				OR = {
					check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var < -3 }
					
					FROM = { is_ai = no }
				}
			}
		}
		
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SRS_northern_war
			add_idea = SRS_northern_clashes
		}
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = SRS_add_delegates_internationalist_4_tt
		
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = { var = internationalists_support_var value = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { var = communards_support_var value = 4 }
		}
		
		FROM = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SRS_northern_war
				add_idea = SRS_northern_clashes
			}
			
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = Ntribes.119
			}
		}

			}

				check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = 2 }
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				
				check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = 3 }
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var > 3 }
				
				FROM = { is_ai = yes }

		}

						level = 1
					}
				}
				
				else = {

						level = 1
					}
				}
			}

country_event = { # Check to include SRS in NTR during the war with a strong opponent
	id = Ntribes.193
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = yes
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						surrender_progress > 0.5
						
						AND = {
							enemies_strength_ratio > 1.5
							surrender_progress > 0.25
						}
						
						AND = {
							enemies_strength_ratio > 2
							surrender_progress > 0.1
						}
					}
					
					NOT = { has_war_with = NTR }
				}
				
				NTR = {
					country_event = Ntribes.149
				}
				
				clr_country_flag = NTR_SRS_integration_check_on
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: self-triggering event Ntribes.193 stopped"
			}
			
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = Ntribes.193
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			clr_country_flag = NTR_SRS_integration_check_on
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: self-triggering event Ntribes.193 stopped"
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Recalculation of overabundance of offsite dockyards and/or complexes
	id = Ntribes.194
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.194" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		add_offsite_building = {
			type = dockyard
			level = 3
		}
		
		add_offsite_building = {
			type = industrial_complex
			level = -2
		}
		
		subtract_from_variable = { NTR_bonus_complexes = 2 }
		
		add_to_variable = { NTR_not_equals_dockyards_calculation = 3 }
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { NTR_not_equals_dockyards_calculation < 4 }
					
					check_variable = { NTR_bonus_complexes < 2 }
				}
			}
			
			country_event = Ntribes.195
		}
		
		else = {
			country_event = Ntribes.194
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Recalculation of lack of offsite dockyards and/or complexes
	id = Ntribes.195
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.195" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		clear_variable = NTR_not_equals_dockyards_calculation
		
		multiply_variable = { NTR_received_offsite_dockyards = -1 }
		
		add_offsite_building = {
			type = dockyards
			level = var:NTR_received_offsite_dockyards
		}
		
		set_variable = { NTR_received_offsite_dockyards = NTR_dockyards_per_agreements }
		
		add_offsite_building = {
			type = dockyards
			level = var:NTR_received_offsite_dockyards
		}
		
		clear_variable = NTR_dockyards_per_agreements
		
		country_event = {
			id = Ntribes.196
			days = 7
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Check for received bonus dockyards
	id = Ntribes.196
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.196" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		set_variable = { NTR_dockyards_per_agreements = 0 }
		
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = NTR_friends_check_for_bonus_dockyards
				
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
				has_government = democratic
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_major = yes
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = event_target:equestria
							tag = event_target:RivFed
						}
					}
					
					add_to_variable = { ROOT.NTR_dockyards_per_agreements = 6 }
				}
				
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { ROOT.NTR_dockyards_per_agreements = 3 }
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.NTR_dockyards_per_agreements = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		divide_variable = { NTR_dockyards_per_agreements = 3 } # 1 dockyard ~ 3 agreement (because of round)
		round_variable = NTR_dockyards_per_agreements
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = NTR_received_offsite_dockyards
					value = NTR_dockyards_per_agreements
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			
			set_variable = { NTR_not_equals_dockyards_calculation = NTR_received_offsite_dockyards }
			subtract_from_variable = { NTR_not_equals_dockyards_calculation = NTR_dockyards_per_agreements }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { NTR_not_equals_dockyards_calculation > 3 }
					
					check_variable = { NTR_bonus_complexes > 1 }
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.194
			}
			
			else = {
				country_event = Ntribes.195
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			clear_variable = NTR_dockyards_per_agreements
			
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.196
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # SRS proposal
	id = Ntribes.250
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.250"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = internationalists_support_var }
			subtract_from_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = communards_support_var }
			
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = NTR_ai_behavior
								option = DEFAULT
							}
						}
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								OR = {
									has_game_rule = {
										rule = NTR_ai_behavior
										option = TOWARDS_REVOLUTION
									}
									
									AND = {
										is_ai = no
										
										has_game_rule = {
											rule = NTR_ai_behavior
											option = RANDOM
										}
										
										has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TOWARDS_REVOLUTION
									}
								}
							}
						}
						
						diplomatic_relation = {
							country = ROOT
							relation = non_aggression_pact
							active = yes
						}
						
						diplomatic_relation = {
							country = ROOT
							relation = guarantee
							active = yes
						}
						
						ROOT = {
							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = FROM
								relation = guarantee
								active = yes
							}
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.202
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.250.t
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_country_flag = NTR_SRS_united_north_request }
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.250.d_a
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_country_flag = NTR_SRS_towards_revolution_request }
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.250.d_b
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = NTR_SRS_united_north_request
						has_country_flag = NTR_SRS_towards_revolution_request
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.250.d_c
	}
	
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # We will build a utopia in the northern wastelands together
		name = Ntribes.250.a
		
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = TOWARDS_REVOLUTION
					}
					
					FROM = {
						is_ai = no
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = RANDOM
						}
						
						has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TOWARDS_REVOLUTION
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				
				check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = 1 } 
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				
				check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = 2 } 
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				
				check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = 3 } 
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				OR = {
					FROM = { has_country_flag = NTR_SRS_towards_revolution_request }
					
					AND = {
						check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var > 3 }
						
						FROM = {
							NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_SRS_united_north_request }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
				FROM = { is_ai = yes }
			}
			
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
		
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
		}
		
		FROM = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				annex_country = {
					target = ROOT
				}
			}
			
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = Ntribes.201
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # We will carry the flame of the revolution together
		name = Ntribes.250.b
		
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = UNITED_NORTH
					}
					
					FROM = {
						is_ai = no
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = RANDOM
						}
						
						has_country_flag = NTR_AI_UNITED_NORTH
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				
				check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = -1 } 
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				
				check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = -2 } 
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				
				check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = -3 } 
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				OR = {
					FROM = { has_country_flag = NTR_SRS_united_north_request }
					
					AND = {
						check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var < -3 }
						
						FROM = {
							NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_SRS_towards_revolution_request }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM
			relation = guarantee
			active = yes
		}
		
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = guarantee
				active = yes
			}
			
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = Ntribes.202
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = Ntribes.312.t
	desc = Ntribes.312.d

		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.312"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { # -PP (-750 - -250)
					check_variable = { party_popularity@neutrality > party_popularity@communism }
				}
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = party_popularity@communism }
				divide_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = party_popularity@neutrality }
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = -1 }
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup = 500 }
			}
			
			else = { # +PP (-250 - +250)
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = party_popularity@neutrality }
				divide_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = party_popularity@communism }
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = -1 }
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup = -500 }
			}
			
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup = NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup = -250 }
			add_political_power = NTR_political_power_after_coup
			
			retire_country_leader = yes #???
			
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Communal Council"
				desc = ""
				picture = "Governor.tga" # portrait #???
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = marxism

			}
		}

country_event = { # Lights in the Polar Night
	id = Ntribes.402
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.402"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { # -PP (-750 - -250)
					check_variable = { party_popularity@neutrality > party_popularity@fascism }
				}
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = party_popularity@fascism }
				divide_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = party_popularity@neutrality }
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = -1 }
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup = 500 }
			}
			
			else = { # +PP (-250 - +250)
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = party_popularity@neutrality }
				divide_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = party_popularity@fascism }
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = -1 }
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup = -500 }
			}
			
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup = NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup = -250 }
			add_political_power = NTR_political_power_after_coup
			
			add_stability = -0.15
			add_war_support = -0.1
			
			add_manpower = -25
			562 = { add_manpower = -80 }
			
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 13451 }
				
				set_nationality = SOL
			}
			
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 13452 }
				
				set_nationality = SOL
			}
			
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = {
					has_id = 13454
				}
				
				set_nationality = SOL
			}
			
			set_cosmetic_tag = NTR_blizzard
			
			set_country_flag = NTR_blizzard_branch
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.402.t
	desc = Ntribes.402.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # Much more to come
		name = Ntribes.402.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.15
			add_war_support = -0.1
			
			add_manpower = -25
			562 = { add_manpower = -80 }
			
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			
			remove_unit_leader = 13451
			remove_unit_leader = 13452
			remove_unit_leader = 13454
			
			set_cosmetic_tag = NTR_blizzard
		}
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = unlock_focuses
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = allow_guarantees
							option = ALWAYS_FREE
						}
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = allow_guarantees
							option = LIMITED
						}
					}
				}
				
				set_rule = { # add AI opinions and strategies #???
					can_guarantee_other_ideologies = yes
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = allow_volunteers
							option = BLOCKED
						}
					}
				}
				
				set_rule = { # add AI opinions and strategies #???
					can_send_volunteers = yes
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = RULE_ALLOW_FACTION
							option = BLOCKED
						}
					}
				}
				
				set_rule = { # add AI opinions and strategies #???
					can_join_factions = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.537"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			add_political_power = 100
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_interest_in_the_outside_world
			
			subtract_from_variable = { var_neutrality_drift = 0.02 }
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_end_the_council = party_popularity@neutrality }
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_end_the_council = -1 }
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = var:NTR_end_the_council
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.537.t
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.537.d_a
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_government = democratic
		}
		
		text = Ntribes.537.d_b
	}
	
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.537.a
		
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = 100
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_interest_in_the_outside_world
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.537.b
		
		trigger = {
			has_government = democratic
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = 100
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_interest_in_the_outside_world
		}
		
		create_corps_commander = { # pegasi
			name = "Libor White"
			picture = "Governor.tga" # portrait #???
			id = 13451
			skill = 2
			attack_skill = 2
			defense_skill = 2
			planning_skill = 1
			logistics_skill = 2
			traits = { infantry_leader infantry_officer }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Part of the World
	id = Ntribes.543
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.543"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			add_political_power = 150
			add_stability = 0.06
			
			set_country_flag = NTR_reintegration_completed
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
				}
				
				clear_variable = NTR_popularity_neutrality_thirds
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = democratic
					}
					
					clear_variable = NTR_popularity_communism_quarter
				}
				
				else = {
					clear_variable = NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				clear_variable = NTR_popularity_communism_quarter
				clear_variable = NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter
			}
			
			clr_country_flag = NTR_integration_in_process #???
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.543.t
	desc = Ntribes.543.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # Let's celebrate with some Sicaemonese wine!
		name = Ntribes.543.a
		
		trigger = {
			has_government = democratic
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = 150
			add_stability = 0.06
			
			set_country_flag = NTR_reintegration_completed
		}
	}
	
	option = { # We only moved towards our destiny.
		name = Ntribes.543.b
		
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = 150
			add_stability = 0.06
			
			set_country_flag = NTR_reintegration_completed
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # In the confrontation, we have benefited
	id = Ntribes.546
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.546"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_var = 0.06 } # 6% from all population
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_factor = party_popularity@ruling_party }
			
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_factor = 1 } # (-1~0) # reverse non-ruling support
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_factor = -0.1 } # 10% from non-ruling supporters
			
			clamp_temp_variable = {
				var = NTR_popularity_factor
				max = 0.03 # max +- 3%
			}
			
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_factor = random }
			
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					add_to_variable = { NTR_popularity_var = NTR_popularity_factor }
				}
				
				60 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { NTR_popularity_var = NTR_popularity_factor }
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = var:NTR_popularity_var
				}
			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = var:NTR_popularity_var
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = var:NTR_popularity_var
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.546.t
	desc = Ntribes.546.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.546.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = var:NTR_popularity_var
				}
			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = var:NTR_popularity_var
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = var:NTR_popularity_var
				}
			}
		}
		
		clear_variable = NTR_popularity_var
	}
}

country_event = { # Fiana is not forgotten
	id = Ntribes.547
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.547"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_var = 0.06 } # 6% from all population
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_factor = party_popularity@democratic }
			
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_factor = 1 } # (-1~0) # reverse communism and neutrality support
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_factor = -0.1 } # 10% from communism and neutrality supporters
			
			clamp_temp_variable = {
				var = NTR_popularity_factor
				max = 0.03 # max +- 3%
			}
			
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_factor = random }
			
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					add_to_variable = { NTR_popularity_var = NTR_popularity_factor }
				}
				
				60 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { NTR_popularity_var = NTR_popularity_factor }
				}
			}
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = var:NTR_popularity_var
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_democratic_check_for_half = party_popularity@democratic }
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_democratic_check_for_half = 0.8 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							focus_progress = {
								focus = NTR_keep_what_is_ours
								progress > 0
							}
							
							focus_progress = {
								focus = NTR_use_guilds_savings
								progress > 0
							}
						}
					}
					
					check_variable = { var_democratic_drift < 0.03 }
					check_variable = { NTR_popularity_democratic_check_for_half > NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter }
				}
				
				add_to_variable = { var_democratic_drift = 0.02 }
				
				set_country_flag = NTR_democrats_debuffs_increased
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.547.t
	desc = Ntribes.547.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = Ntribes.547.a
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = var:NTR_popularity_var
			}
		}
		
		clear_variable = NTR_popularity_var
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = NTR_democrats_debuffs_increased
			}
			
			custom_effect_tooltip = NTR_democratic_influence_increased_tooltip
			
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = NTR_democrats_debuffs_increased
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Tribal Council is gathering more and more supporters
	id = Ntribes.549
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.549"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_var = 0.06 } # 6% from all population
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_factor = party_popularity@neutrality }
			
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_factor = 1 } # (-1~0) # reverse democracy and communism support
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_factor = -0.1 } # 10% from democracy and communism supporters
			
			clamp_temp_variable = {
				var = NTR_popularity_factor
				max = 0.03 # max +- 3%
			}
			
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_factor = random }
			
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					add_to_variable = { NTR_popularity_var = NTR_popularity_factor }
				}
				
				60 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { NTR_popularity_var = NTR_popularity_factor }
				}
			}
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = var:NTR_popularity_var
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_check_for_quarter = party_popularity@neutrality }
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_check_for_quarter = 0.8 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							focus_progress = {
								focus = NTR_new_regional_administration
								progress > 0
							}
							
							focus_progress = {
								focus = NTR_transforming_the_old_traditions
								progress > 0
							}
						}
					}
					
					has_idea = NTR_interest_in_the_outside_world
					check_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_check_for_quarter > NTR_popularity_neutrality_thirds }
				}
				
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = NTR_interest_in_the_outside_world
					add_idea = NTR_tensions_between_the_new_and_the_old
				}
				
				add_to_variable = { var_neutrality_drift = 0.02 }
				
				set_country_flag = NTR_neutrality_debuffs_increased
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.549.t

	option = {

				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = var:NTR_popularity_var
			}
		}
		
		clear_variable = NTR_popularity_var
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = NTR_neutrality_debuffs_increased
			}
			
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = NTR_interest_in_the_outside_world
					add_idea = NTR_tensions_between_the_new_and_the_old
				}
			}
			
			custom_effect_tooltip = NTR_neutrality_influence_increased_tooltip
			
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = NTR_neutrality_debuffs_increased
			}

	}

country_event = { # Request from "The Palace"
	id = Ntribes.550
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.550"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = internationalists_support_var }
			subtract_from_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = communards_support_var }
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.550.t
	desc = Ntribes.550.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # While the battle is going on, sabotage groups will be able to pass
		name = Ntribes.550.a
		
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_border_war_with = NTR }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				
				check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = 1 }
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				
				check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = 2 }
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				
				check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var = 3 }
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				
				check_variable = { communards_vs_internationalists_support_var > 3 }
			}
		}
		
		add_political_power = -50
		
		start_border_war = {
			change_state_after_war = no
			
			attacker = {
				state = 561
				num_provinces = 6
				on_win = srs_borderwar.3 # will be unique
				on_lose = srs_borderwar.4 # will be unique
				on_cancel = srs_borderwar.5 # will be unique

					id = Ntribes.560
					days = 7
					random = 28
				}
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Will we vote?
		name = Ntribes.562.c
		
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = NTR_ai_behavior
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = NTR_ai_behavior
					option = RANDOM
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = NTR_ai_behavior
					option = DEFAULT
				}
			}
			
			custom_effect_tooltip = NTR_play_with_system
			
			effect_tooltip = {
				random_list = {
					40 = {
						add_war_support = -0.025
					}
					
					60 = {
						add_political_power = -25
						add_stability = -0.025
						add_war_support = 0.025
					}
				}
			}
			
			hidden_effect = {
				NTR_calculate_political_path_if_necessary = yes
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
							has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE
						}
					}
					
					add_war_support = -0.025
					
					country_event = {
						id = Ntribes.563
						days = 7
						random = 28
					}
				}
				
				else = {
					add_political_power = -25
					add_stability = -0.025
					add_war_support = 0.025
					
					country_event = {
						id = Ntribes.560
						days = 7
						random = 28
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = VEDINA
					}
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = TRADE
					}
					
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE
				}
				
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_war_support = -0.025
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_political_power = -25
					add_stability = -0.025
					add_war_support = 0.025
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Clashing in the Woods
	id = Ntribes.563
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.563"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.025
			
			add_manpower = -80
			
			562 = {
				add_manpower = -260
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_ai = no
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = RANDOM
						}
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_country_flag = NTR_AI_UNITED_NORTH
								has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TOWARDS_REVOLUTION
							}
						}
						
						add_political_power = 25
					}
					
					else = {
						add_war_support = -0.025
					}
				}
				
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADITIONS
							has_country_flag = NTR_AI_SYNTHESIS
						}
					}
					
					add_political_power = -25
					add_war_support = -0.025
				}
			}
			
			add_to_variable = { var_communism_drift = 0.01 }
			
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.560
				days = 7
				random = 28
			}
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.563.t
	desc = Ntribes.563.d

					rule = NTR_ai_behavior
					option = UNITED_NORTH
				}
				
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = NTR_ai_behavior
					option = TOWARDS_REVOLUTION
				}
				
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NTR_ai_behavior
						option = RANDOM
					}
				}
				
				has_country_flag = NTR_AI_UNITED_NORTH
				has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TOWARDS_REVOLUTION
			}
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.025
			
			add_manpower = -80
			
			562 = {
				add_manpower = -260
			}
		}
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = NTR_communism_influence_increased_tooltip
	}

country_event = { # A Pivotal Dress-choice
	id = Ntribes.568
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.568"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_ai = no
						
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = NTR_ai_behavior
							option = RANDOM
						}
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_country_flag = NTR_AI_UNITED_NORTH
								has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TOWARDS_REVOLUTION
							}
						}
						
						add_political_power = -50
						add_stability = -0.025
						
						country_event = {
							id = Ntribes.577
							days = 7
							random = 28
						}
					}
					
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
								has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE
							}
						}
						
						add_political_power = -50
						add_war_support = -0.025
						
						country_event = {
							id = Ntribes.572
							days = 7
							random = 28
						}
					}

							days = 7

					}

					}

					is_ai = no

					}
				}

					rule = NTR_ai_behavior

			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = NTR_ai_behavior
					option = DEFAULT
				}
			}
			
			custom_effect_tooltip = NTR_play_with_system
			
			effect_tooltip = {
				random_list = {
					50 = {
						add_political_power = 100
						add_stability = 0.05
						
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = democratic
							popularity = 0.05
						}
					}
					
					50 = {
						add_political_power = 150
						add_stability = 0.025
						
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = democratic
							popularity = 0.025
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
								has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE
								has_country_flag = NTR_AI_UNITED_NORTH
								has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TOWARDS_REVOLUTION
								has_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADITIONS
								has_country_flag = NTR_AI_SYNTHESIS
							}
						}
					}
					
					random_list = {
						50 = { set_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA }
						50 = { set_country_flag = NTR_AI_TRADE }
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
					}
					
					add_political_power = 100
					add_stability = 0.05
					
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = democratic
						popularity = 0.05
					}
				}
				
				else = {
					add_political_power = 150
					add_stability = 0.025
					
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = democratic
						popularity = 0.025
					}
					
					set_country_flag = NTR_SRS_more_peaceful_politics
				}
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_VEDINA
				}
				
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_political_power = 100
					add_stability = 0.05
					
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = democratic
						popularity = 0.05
					}
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_political_power = 150
					add_stability = 0.025
					
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = democratic
						popularity = 0.025
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = -0.05
			}
		}
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = NTR_communism_influence_reduced_tooltip
	}
}

country_event = { # The Sudden Coup
	id = Ntribes.579
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.579"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { # -PP (-750 - -250)
					check_variable = { party_popularity@democratic > party_popularity@communism }
				}
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = party_popularity@communism }
				divide_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = party_popularity@democratic }
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = -1 }
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup = 500 }
			}
			
			else = { # +PP (-250 - +250)
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = party_popularity@democratic }
				divide_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = party_popularity@communism }
				add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier = -1 }
				
				set_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup = -500 }
			}
			
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup = NTR_political_power_after_coup_multiplier }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_political_power_after_coup = -250 }
			add_political_power = NTR_political_power_after_coup
			
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.075
			}
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_ivor_eklund
			
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NTR_adam_watershed
				add_idea = NTR_ivor_eklund
			}
			
			remove_ideas = NTR_communist_influence
			clear_variable = var_communism_drift
			
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Adam Watershed" # Chairman of General National Congress
				desc = ""
				picture = "Governor.tga" # portrait #???
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = leninism
				traits = { national_hero }
			}

				name = "Adam Watershed"
				picture = "Governor.tga" # portrait #???
				id = 13457
				skill = 3
				attack_skill = 3
				defense_skill = 2
				planning_skill = 2
				logistics_skill = 3
				traits = { war_hero organisational_leader old_guard }
			}
			
			create_corps_commander = { # to advisor someday #???

				picture = "Blind_archer.tga"
				id = 13458
				skill = 2
				attack_skill = 1
				defense_skill = 3
				planning_skill = 1
				logistics_skill = 2
				traits = { war_hero adaptable old_guard blind }
			}
			
			add_ideas = NTR_defiant_harmonic_tribes
			set_variable = { var_democratic_drift = 0.04 }
			add_NTR_harmonic_tribes_effects = yes
			
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = {
					has_id = 13450
				}
				
				set_nationality = SOL
			}
			
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SRS
				}
				
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
			
			NTR_remove_demilitarized_zones = yes
			
			set_cosmetic_tag = NTR_SRS_faction
			
			country_event = Ntribes.595
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.579.t
	desc = Ntribes.579.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # The Red Banner Rises in the North

				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			
			add_popularity = {

				popularity = 0.075
			}
			
			create_country_leader = {

				desc = ""
				picture = "Governor.tga" # portrait #???
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = leninism
				traits = { national_hero }
			}

				id = 13457
				skill = 3
				attack_skill = 3
				defense_skill = 2
				planning_skill = 2
				logistics_skill = 3

			}

			clear_variable = NTR_democratic_emergency_support

country_event = { #	Check for decreasing of ideological ideas
	id = Ntribes.592
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.592" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_reintegration_check_for_half = party_popularity@neutrality }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_reintegration_check_for_half = party_popularity@communism }
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_check_for_two_thirds_and_trirds = party_popularity@neutrality }
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_check_for_two_thirds_and_trirds = 0.67 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NTR_popularity_neutrality_check_for_two_thirds_and_trirds
						value = NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.541
			}
			
			divide_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_check_for_two_thirds_and_trirds = 2 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NTR_popularity_neutrality_check_for_two_thirds_and_trirds
						value = NTR_popularity_neutrality_thirds
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.540
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_communism_check_for_quarter = party_popularity@communism }
			divide_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_communism_check_for_quarter = 2 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NTR_popularity_communism_check_for_quarter
						value = NTR_popularity_communism_quarter
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						
						NOT = {
							state = 574
							state = 677
						}
					}
					
					save_global_event_target_as = NTR_commie_event_target
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.539
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_reintegration_check_for_half = party_popularity@neutrality }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_reintegration_check_for_half = party_popularity@democratic }
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_check_for_two_thirds_and_trirds = party_popularity@neutrality }
			multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_check_for_two_thirds_and_trirds = 0.67 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = NTR_popularity_neutrality_check_for_two_thirds_and_trirds
							value = NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
					
					country_event = Ntribes.541
				}
			}
			
			divide_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_check_for_two_thirds_and_trirds = 2 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NTR_popularity_neutrality_check_for_two_thirds_and_trirds
						value = NTR_popularity_neutrality_thirds
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.540
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_democratic_check_for_quarter = party_popularity@democratic }
			divide_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_democratic_check_for_quarter = 2 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NTR_popularity_democratic_check_for_quarter
						value = NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.538
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_reintegration_check_for_half = party_popularity@democratic }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_reintegration_check_for_half = party_popularity@communism }
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_democratic_check_for_quarter = party_popularity@democratic }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NTR_popularity_democratic_check_for_quarter
						value = NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.538
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { NTR_popularity_communism_check_for_quarter = party_popularity@communism }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NTR_popularity_communism_check_for_quarter
						value = NTR_popularity_communism_quarter
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						
						NOT = {
							state = 574
							state = 677
						}
					}
					
					save_global_event_target_as = NTR_commie_event_target
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.539
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = NTR_reintegration_check_for_half
					value = NTR_reintegration_half
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.545
			}
			
			else = {
				country_event = Ntribes.544
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { NTR_reintegration_check_for_half < 0.1 }
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.543
			}
			
			else = {
				country_event = Ntribes.542
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Bypassing the autistic paradox decision code
	id = Ntribes.593
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.593" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = NTR_popularity_var
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = NTR_popularity_var
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = NTR_popularity_var
			}
		}
		
		clear_variable = NTR_popularity_var
		clear_variable = NTR_popularity_factor
		
		country_event = Ntribes.592
	}
}

country_event = { # Check for calling anti-government events
	id = Ntribes.594
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.594" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = NTR_integration_in_process
	}
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = { # can be improved #???
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.4 }
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				random_list = {
					30 = { # neu+
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {
								check_variable = { party_popularity@neutrality = 0 }
								
								AND = {
									focus_progress = {
										focus = NTR_new_regional_administration
										progress > 0
									}
									NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_new_regional_administration }
								}
							}
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.549
					}
					
					30 = { # com+
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {
								check_variable = { party_popularity@communism = 0 }
								
								AND = {
									focus_progress = {
										focus = NTR_guilds_will_do_their_part
										progress > 0
									}
									NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_guilds_will_do_their_part }
								}
							}
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.548
					}
					
					40 = {
						modifier = {
							add = -10
							
							check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.6 }
						}
						
						modifier = {
							add = -10
							
							check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.8 }
						}
						
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {
								check_variable = { party_popularity@neutrality = 0 }
								check_variable = { party_popularity@communism = 0 }
							}
						}
						
						set_temp_variable = { NTR_ruling_party_multiplier = 1 }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { NTR_ruling_party_multiplier = party_popularity@ruling_party }
						
						set_temp_variable = { NTR_ruling_party_ratio = 1 }
						divide_temp_variable = { NTR_ruling_party_ratio = NTR_ruling_party_multiplier }
						multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_ruling_party_ratio = 10 }
						
						set_variable = { NTR_communism_emergency_support = party_popularity@communism }
						multiply_variable = { NTR_communism_emergency_support = NTR_ruling_party_multiplier }
						round_variable = NTR_communism_emergency_support
						
						set_variable = { NTR_neutrality_emergency_support = party_popularity@neutrality }
						divide_variable = { NTR_neutrality_emergency_support = NTR_ruling_party_multiplier }
						round_variable = NTR_neutrality_emergency_support
						
						activate_mission = NTR_clashes_in_the_north
					}
				}
			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				random_list = {
					30 = { # neu+
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {
								check_variable = { party_popularity@neutrality = 0 }
								
								AND = {
									focus_progress = {
										focus = NTR_transforming_the_old_traditions
										progress > 0
									}
									NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_transforming_the_old_traditions }
								}
							}
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.549
					}
					
					30 = { # dem+
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {
								check_variable = { party_popularity@democratic = 0 }
								
								AND = {
									focus_progress = {
										focus = NTR_transforming_the_old_traditions
										progress > 0
									}
									NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_use_guilds_savings }
								}
							}
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.547
					}
					
					40 = {
						modifier = {
							add = -10
							
							check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.6 }
						}
						
						modifier = {
							add = -10
							
							check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.8 }
						}
						
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {
								check_variable = { party_popularity@neutrality = 0 }
								check_variable = { party_popularity@democratic = 0 }
							}
						}
						
						set_variable = { NTR_democratic_emergency_support = party_popularity@democratic }
						divide_variable = { NTR_democratic_emergency_support = party_popularity@neutrality }
						
						set_variable = { NTR_neutrality_emergency_support = party_popularity@neutrality }
						divide_variable = { NTR_neutrality_emergency_support = party_popularity@democratic }
						
						activate_mission = NTR_clashes_in_the_north
					}
				}
			}
			
			else = {

					30 = { # com+
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {

								AND = {
									focus_progress = {
										focus = NTR_reasserting_tribal_authority
										progress > 0
									}
									NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_reasserting_tribal_authority }
								}
							}
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.548
					}
					
					30 = { # dem+
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							
							OR = {
								check_variable = { party_popularity@democratic = 0 }
								
								AND = {
									focus_progress = {
										focus = NTR_keep_what_is_ours
										progress > 0
									}
									NOT = { has_completed_focus = NTR_keep_what_is_ours }
								}
							}
						}
						
						country_event = Ntribes.547
					}
					
					40 = {

							add = -10

						set_variable = { NTR_democratic_emergency_support = party_popularity@democratic }

country_event = { #	Calculation of variables for reintegration
	id = Ntribes.595
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.595" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds = party_popularity@neutrality }
			multiply_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds = 0.67 }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half = party_popularity@neutrality }
			divide_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half = 2 }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds = NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds }
			divide_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_thirds = 2 }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_communism_quarter = party_popularity@communism }
			divide_variable = { NTR_popularity_communism_quarter = 2 }
			
			add_to_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half = NTR_popularity_communism_quarter }
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds = party_popularity@neutrality }
			multiply_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds = 0.67 }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half = party_popularity@neutrality }
			divide_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half = 2 }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds = NTR_popularity_neutrality_two_thirds }
			divide_variable = { NTR_popularity_neutrality_thirds = 2 }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter = party_popularity@democratic }
			divide_variable = { NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter = 2 }
			
			add_to_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half = NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter }
		}
		
		else = {
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter = party_popularity@democratic }
			divide_variable = { NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter = 2 }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half = NTR_popularity_democratic_quarter }
			
			set_variable = { NTR_popularity_communism_quarter = party_popularity@communism }
			divide_variable = { NTR_popularity_communism_quarter = 2 }
			
			add_to_variable = { NTR_reintegration_half = NTR_popularity_communism_quarter }
		}
		
		set_country_flag = NTR_integration_in_process #???
		
		country_event = { #???
			id = Ntribes.594
			days = 45
			random = 360
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Self-triggering check for NTR_harmonic_influence modifier
	id = Ntribes.597
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = NTR_harmonic_influence
				}
			}
			
			remove_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = NTR_harmonic_influence
			}
			
			add_NTR_harmonic_tribes_effects = yes
			
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.597
				days = 1
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: self-triggering event Ntribes.597 stopped"
		}
	}
}
