country_event = { #	Increase poverty (up agrarian and pre-industrial society)
	id = Ntribes.906
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.906"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = -0.05
				}
			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = -0.05
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				add_political_power = -50
				add_stability = -0.025
			}
			
			increase_poverty = yes
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.906.t
	desc = Ntribes.906.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = { # Bad news
		name = Ntribes.906.a

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = -0.05
				}
			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = -0.05
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				add_political_power = -50
				add_stability = -0.025
			}
			
			NTR_increase_poverty_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Refugees from the East
	id = Ntribes.908
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.908"
		
		hidden_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.05
			
			set_variable = { divider = -10 }
			set_variable = { randomizer = 0.3 }
			set_variable = { rounder = 100 }
			
			DED = {
				save_current_manpower = yes
			}
			
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 565
						state = 566
						state = 428
					}
				}
				
				set_variable = { population = state_population }
				population_calculator_multifunctional = yes
				population_calculation_for_sum = yes
			}
			
			DED = {
				restore_previous_manpower = yes
			}
			
			multiply_variable = { population_sum = -1 }
			
			set_variable = { divider = 2 }
			set_variable = { randomizer = 0.2 }
			set_variable = { rounder = 100 }
			
			set_variable = { population = population_sum }
			population_calculator_multifunctional = yes
			subtract_from_variable = { population_sum = population }
			
			population_calculator_cleaner = yes
			
			save_current_manpower = yes
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { population_sum > population }
				}
				
				573 = {
					add_manpower = var:ROOT.population_sum
				}
				
				563 = {
					add_manpower = var:ROOT.population
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				573 = {
					add_manpower = var:ROOT.population
				}
				
				563 = {
					add_manpower = var:ROOT.population_sum
				}
			}
			
			restore_previous_manpower = yes
		}
	}
	
	title = Ntribes.908.t
	desc = Ntribes.908.d
	#picture = 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { # Send healers and food east to help however we can

		trigger = {
			has_government = democratic
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.05
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { population_sum > population }
				}
				
				573 = {
					add_manpower = var:ROOT.population_sum
				}
				
				563 = {
					add_manpower = var:ROOT.population
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				573 = {
					add_manpower = var:ROOT.population
				}
				
				563 = {
					add_manpower = var:ROOT.population_sum
				}
			}
		}
		
		population_clr_junk = yes
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = Ntribes.909
				days = 3
				random = 24
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # They are welcome here

country_event = { # Calculation for frosen_seas icebreakers_ratio change
	id = Ntribes.992
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		set_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_reverse_ratio = num_equipment@icebreaker }
		divide_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_reverse_ratio = NTR_icebreakers_required }
		
		clamp_variable = {
			var = NTR_icebreakers_reverse_ratio
			max = 1
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_reverse_ratio < 1 }
			}
			
			multiply_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_reverse_ratio = -1 }
			add_to_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_reverse_ratio = 1 }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = frosen_seas
					}
					
					NOT = { has_idea = closed_economy }
				}
				
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = frosen_seas
				}
				
				add_frosen_seas_modifier_effects = yes
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = frosen_seas
					}
				}
				
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = frosen_seas
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Self-triggering check for frosen_seas modifier
	id = Ntribes.993
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		set_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_required = modifier@min_export }
		multiply_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_required = 20 }
		
		set_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp = resource_exported@oil }
		add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp = resource_exported@aluminium }
		add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp = resource_exported@rubber }
		add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp = resource_exported@tungsten }
		add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp = resource_exported@steel }
		add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp = resource_exported@chromium }
		add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp = resource_exported@crystals }
		
		add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp = resource_imported@oil }
		add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp = resource_imported@aluminium }
		add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp = resource_imported@rubber }
		add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp = resource_imported@tungsten }
		add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp = resource_imported@steel }
		add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp = resource_imported@chromium }
		add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp = resource_imported@crystals }
		
		divide_temp_variable = { NTR_resources_temp = 8 }
		add_to_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_required = NTR_resources_temp }
		
		set_temp_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp = 0 }
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = NTR_FAT_FAW_Tspirit }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = NTR_MNC_Tspirit }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = NTR_HLR_Tspirit }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = NTR_VED_Tspirit }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = NTR_PNG_Tspirit }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = NTR_NCH_Tspirit }
			add_to_temp_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp = 1 }
		}
		
		multiply_temp_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp = 3 }
		add_to_variable = { NTR_icebreakers_required = NTR_icebreakers_for_agreements_neighbors_temp }
		
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				has_government = democratic
				
				has_country_flag = NTR_friends_check_for_bonus_dockyards
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_major = yes
				}
				
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.NTR_icebreakers_required = 3 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_subject = no
				}
				
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.NTR_icebreakers_required = 2 }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.NTR_icebreakers_required = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		round_variable = NTR_icebreakers_required
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { global.month < 6 }
					check_variable = { global.month > 9 }
				}
			}
			
			country_event = Ntribes.992
		}
		
		else = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: self-triggering event Ntribes.993 stopped"
		}
		
		country_event = {
			id = Ntribes.993
			days = 7
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Check for owns_state flags
	id = Ntribes.999
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.999" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_of = {
						array = SRS.core_states
						
						var:v = {
							NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_owns_SRS_cores_flag }
				}
				
				set_country_flag = NTR_owns_SRS_cores_flag
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_of = {
							array = VED.core_states
							
							var:v = {
								NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_owns_SRS_VED_cores_flag }
					}
					
					set_country_flag = NTR_owns_SRS_VED_cores_flag
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							any_of = {
								array = HAU.core_states
								
								var:v = {
									NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_owns_SRS_VED_HAU_cores_flag }
						}
						
						set_country_flag = NTR_owns_SRS_VED_HAU_cores_flag
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Ist iteration of the calculations for AI Military Behavior Flags
	id = Ntribes.1000
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.1000"
		
		clr_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_LOW
		clr_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_MEDIUM
		clr_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_HIGH
		clr_country_flag = NTR_AI_NAVY_LOW
		clr_country_flag = NTR_AI_NAVY_MEDIUM
		clr_country_flag = NTR_AI_NAVY_HIGH
	}
	
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = { # just for remove further unnecessary checks in the events
				num_faction_members > 1
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_war = yes
						
						any_allied_country = {
							has_war = yes
						}
					}
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.1004
			}
			
			else = {
				country_event = Ntribes.1003
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war = yes
				}
				
				country_event = Ntribes.1002
			}
			
			else = {
				country_event = Ntribes.1001
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # IInd iteration of the calculations for AI Military Behavior Flags - Prepare for war (solo)
	id = Ntribes.1001
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.1001"
		
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_or_is_justifying_wargoal_against_ROOT = yes
			}
			
			set_country_flag = NTR_potential_enemy
		}
	}
	
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_other_country = {
					exists = yes
					
					has_country_flag = NTR_potential_enemy
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_other_country = {
						has_country_flag = NTR_potential_enemy
						
						OR = {
							is_neighbor_of = ROOT
							
							any_allied_country = {
								is_neighbor_of = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}
				
				set_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_MEDIUM
			}
			
			else = {
				set_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_LOW
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_other_country = {
						has_country_flag = NTR_potential_enemy
						
						OR = {
							any_state = {
								is_controlled_by = PREV
								is_coastal = yes
							}
							
							any_allied_country = {
								any_state = {
									is_controlled_by = PREV
									is_coastal = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_LOW
					}
					
					set_country_flag = NTR_AI_NAVY_MEDIUM
				}
				
				else = {
					set_country_flag = NTR_AI_NAVY_LOW
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_MEDIUM
					}
					
					clr_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_MEDIUM
					set_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_HIGH
				}
			}
		}
		
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = NTR_potential_enemy
			}
			
			clr_country_flag = NTR_potential_enemy
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # IIIrd iteration of the calculations for AI Military Behavior Flags - Has war (solo)
	id = Ntribes.1002
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.1002" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_enemy_country = {
					OR = {
						is_neighbor_of = ROOT
						
						any_allied_country = {
							is_neighbor_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			set_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_HIGH
		}
		
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_enemy_country = {
						any_neighbor_country = {
							has_war_with = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				
				set_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_MEDIUM
			}
			
			else = {
				set_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_LOW
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_enemy_country = {
					OR = {
						any_state = {
							is_controlled_by = PREV
							is_coastal = yes
						}
						
						any_allied_country = {
							any_state = {
								is_controlled_by = PREV
								is_coastal = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_LOW
				}
				
				set_country_flag = NTR_AI_NAVY_HIGH
			}
			
			else = {
				set_country_flag = NTR_AI_NAVY_MEDIUM
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			set_country_flag = NTR_AI_NAVY_LOW
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_MEDIUM
				}
				
				clr_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_MEDIUM
				set_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_HIGH
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # IInd iteration of the calculations for AI Military Behavior Flags - Prepare for war (ally)
	id = Ntribes.1003
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.1003"
		
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				
				has_or_is_justifying_wargoal_against_ROOT = yes
			}
			
			set_country_flag = NTR_potential_enemy
		}
		
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = allies
			
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					exists = yes
					
					OR = {
						has_wargoal_against = PREV
						is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
						
						PREV = {
							OR = {
								has_wargoal_against = PREV
								is_justifying_wargoal_against = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = NTR_potential_enemy }
					}
					
					set_country_flag = NTR_potential_enemy
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_other_country = {
					exists = yes
					
					has_country_flag = NTR_potential_enemy
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_allied_country = {
						any_other_country = {
							has_country_flag = NTR_potential_enemy
							
							OR = {
								is_neighbor_of = ROOT
								is_neighbor_of = PREV
								
								any_allied_country = {
									OR = {
										is_neighbor_of = ROOT
										is_neighbor_of = PREV
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				
				set_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_MEDIUM
			}
			
			else = {
				set_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_LOW
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_other_country = {
						has_country_flag = NTR_potential_enemy
						
						OR = {
							any_state = {
								is_controlled_by = PREV
								is_coastal = yes
							}
							
							any_allied_country = {
								any_state = {
									is_controlled_by = PREV
									is_coastal = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_LOW
					}
					
					set_country_flag = NTR_AI_NAVY_MEDIUM
				}
				
				else = {
					set_country_flag = NTR_AI_NAVY_LOW
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_MEDIUM
					}
					
					clr_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_MEDIUM
					set_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_HIGH
				}
			}
		}
		
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = NTR_potential_enemy
			}
			
			clr_country_flag = NTR_potential_enemy
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # IIIrd iteration of the calculations for AI Military Behavior Flags - Has war (ally)
	id = Ntribes.1004
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Ntribes.1004" }
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_allied_country = {
					any_enemy_country = {
						OR = {
							is_neighbor_of = ROOT
							is_neighbor_of = PREV
							
							any_allied_country = {
								OR = {
									is_neighbor_of = ROOT
									is_neighbor_of = PREV
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			set_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_HIGH
		}
		
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_allied_country = {
						any_enemy_country = {
							any_neighbor_country = {
								OR = {
									has_war_with = PREV
									has_war_with = PREV.PREV
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				
				set_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_MEDIUM
			}
			
			else = {
				set_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_LOW
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_enemy_country = {
					OR = {
						any_state = {
							is_controlled_by = PREV
							is_coastal = yes
						}
						
						any_allied_country = {
							any_state = {
								is_controlled_by = PREV
								is_coastal = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_LOW
				}
				
				set_country_flag = NTR_AI_NAVY_HIGH
			}
			
			else = {
				set_country_flag = NTR_AI_NAVY_MEDIUM
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			set_country_flag = NTR_AI_NAVY_LOW
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_MEDIUM
				}
				
				clr_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_MEDIUM
				set_country_flag = NTR_AI_ARMY_HIGH
			}
		}
	}
}
